Standard GUI template for generating forms to run on a PC.
The template includes an iconic MDI toolbar, with tool tips  help, and a pre-defined set of CG$ visual attributes.

/* CGNV$CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS */
/* Close any open windows in the form */
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_enter_query := FALSE;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.MODE') = 'ENTER-QUERY') THEN
    exit_form;
  ELSE
    CGNV$.CLOSE_ALL_WINDOWS(name_in('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'));
  END IF;
END;

  END IF;
END;

/* CGYR$SET_DATE_FORMAT */
/* Establish Single Standard Format Mask with 4-digit-year element */
BEGIN
  set_application_property(DATE_FORMAT_COMPATIBILITY_MODE, '5.0');
  set_application_property(PLSQL_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  set_application_property(BUILTIN_DATE_FORMAT, 'YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS');
  forms_ddl('ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = ''YYYY/MM/DD HH24:MI:SS''');
END;

/* CGNV$PRE_FORM_NAVCCF */
/* Set if we want to close child forms as well as child windows */
  DECLARE
  rg_id RECORDGROUP;
  gc_type GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_name GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_parent GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_tag GROUPCOLUMN;
  gc_extra GROUPCOLUMN;
BEGIN
  CGNV$.nav_opening_wnd := FALSE;
  :global.CGNV_last_closed_form := '0';
  :global.CGNV_child_form := find_form(get_application_property(FORM_NAME)).id;
  rg_id := create_group('CGSH$FORM_OBJECTS');
  gc_type := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_TYPE', CHAR_COLUMN, 2);
  gc_name := add_group_column(rg_id, 'OBJECT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_parent := add_group_column(rg_id, 'PARENT_NAME', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_tag := add_group_column(rg_id, 'ITEM_TAG', CHAR_COLUMN, 40);
  gc_extra := add_group_column(rg_id, 'EXTRA_TEXT', CHAR_COLUMN, 240);
  add_group_row(rg_id, 1);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 1, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 1, 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 1, '');
  add_group_row(rg_id, 2);
  set_group_char_cell(gc_type, 2, 'WN');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_name, 2, 'WINDOW');
  set_group_char_cell(gc_parent, 2, '');
END;

/* CGGN$GET_DATE_AND_USER */
/* Get the current user and date; store in items for general use */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    CURSOR C IS
      SELECT  SYSDATE, USER
      FROM    SYS.DUAL;
  BEGIN
    OPEN C;
    FETCH C
    INTO    :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE, :PARAMETER.CGU$USER;
    IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C;
      MESSAGE('Internal Error: No row in table SYS.DUAL');
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C;
  END;
END;

/*CGAP$TES_SEQUENCE_BEFORE*/
DECLARE
   v_current_block_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   c_last_block_name  CONSTANT v_current_block_name% TYPE :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, last_block );

   v_current_item_name  pkg_mylib_form_types. subtyp_obj_name;
   v_current_item_id  ITEM;
   v_last_item_name  v_current_item_name% TYPE;

BEGIN

   v_current_block_name :=
      Get_Form_Property ( :system.current_form, first_block );
   << Loop_All_Blocks >>
   LOOP
      IF Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, records_displayed ) > 1
      THEN

         v_last_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, last_item );

         v_current_item_name :=
            Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, first_item );
         << Loop_All_Block_Items >>
         LOOP
         	  v_current_item_id :=
         	     Find_Item
            	    ( v_current_block_name || '.' || v_current_item_name );

            IF Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, displayed ) = 'TRUE' AND
             	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id, item_canvas ) IS NOT NULL AND
            	 Get_Item_Property
            	    ( v_current_item_id,
                    records_displayed ) > 1 -- displayed > once; this property is NEVER 0 at runtime;
            THEN
               Set_Item_Property
                  ( v_current_item_id,
                    current_record_attribute,
                    'CG$CURRENT_RECORD' ); -- "safe" to hard-code name bec this is a STD visual attr.;
            END IF;

         EXIT WHEN v_current_item_name = v_last_item_name;
            v_current_item_name :=
               Get_Item_Property ( v_current_item_id, nextitem );

         END LOOP Loop_All_Block_Items;

      END IF;

   EXIT WHEN v_current_block_name = c_last_block_name;
      v_current_block_name :=
         Get_Block_Property ( v_current_block_name, nextblock );

   END LOOP Loop_All_Blocks;
END;

/* CGLY$COPY_USER_DATE */
/* Values from USER and DATE items on content canvas 0 in the control */
/* block will be \"fired\" to all other USER and DATE items           */
/* on other content canvas.                                           */
BEGIN
  CGBS2$.SET_COORD_STYLE( 'P' );
  CGBS2$.SET_QRY_ON_ENTRY( 'Y' );
  CGBS2$.SET_NAV_FROM_BLOCK( 'WB_HAULER_HDR' );
  :CG$CTRL.CG$DT := :PARAMETER.CGU$SYSDATE;
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'CG$CTRL.CG$US');
END;

/* CGBS$KEY_ENTQRY_FRM */
/* Check if query is allowed to avoid unnecessary coordination */
BEGIN
  IF (get_block_property( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK'), QUERY_ALLOWED) = 'FALSE') THEN
    MESSAGE('Error: Query not allowed in this block');
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  CGBS$.DO_KEYQRY( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK'), 'ENTER_QUERY', name_in('SYSTEM.MODE'));
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRBLK_FRM */
/* Perform checks prior to clearing block */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.BLOCK_STATUS') = 'CHANGED' OR CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_block( NO_VALIDATE );
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes
   - Execution Hierarchy                             Override
   * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                      Yes
   - 'Keyboard Help' Text                            
   - Trigger Steps                                   
   ----------
   * Name                                            KEY-CLRREC
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   - Trigger Style                                   PL/SQL
   * Trigger Text                                    

/* CGBS$KEY_CLRREC */
/* Avoid clearing details if current row is new and invalid */
BEGIN
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_RECORD_DIRTY(name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK')) ) THEN
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
  END IF;
  IF ( CGBS2$.IS_COMMIT_NEEDED( name_in('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_BLOCK') ) ) THEN
    CGBS2$.DO_COMMIT_DIALOGUE;
  END IF;
  clear_record;
END;

/* CGBS$TOGGLE_QUERY_MODE */
/* This changes the mode of block synchronization so that if it is */
/* currently ON, then it is changed to OFF, and vice-versa.        */
/* It also queries the dependent blocks as appropriate for the     */
/* new mode.                                                       */
BEGIN
  CGBS$TOGGLE( :GLOBAL.CG$QUERY_MODE );
END;
   - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                        Yes

     if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED )='TRUE' then
        set_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED, PROPERTY_FALSE);
     end if;
  else
     if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED )='FALSE' then
        set_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED, PROPERTY_TRUE);
     end if;
  end if;
end;

/* CGWH$SET_AUDIT_UPD_FLDS */
/* Set the date and/or user updated items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'WB_HAULER_HDR.MODIFIED_BY');
  copy(SYSDATE, 'WB_HAULER_HDR.DT_MODIFIED');
END;

declare
   vContainer varchar2(20);
begin
   select container_code
   into   vContainer
   from   wb_hauler_hdr
   where  waybill_no = :wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_no;

   if :wb_hauler_hdr.container_code is null and vContainer is not null then
      update wb_containers 
      set    status = 'EM',
             loading_no = null,
             fcl_waybill_no = null
      where  container_code = vContainer;
   elsif :wb_hauler_hdr.container_code is not null and vContainer is not null then
      update wb_containers 
      set    status = 'EM',
             loading_no = null,
             fcl_waybill_no = null
      where  container_code = vContainer;
   
      update wb_containers  
      set    status = 'OP',
             loading_no = null,
             fcl_waybill_no = :wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_no
      where  container_code = :wb_hauler_hdr.container_code;
   elsif :wb_hauler_hdr.container_code is not null and vContainer is null then
      update wb_containers  
      set    status = 'OP',
             loading_no = null,
             fcl_waybill_no = :wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_no
      where  container_code = :wb_hauler_hdr.container_code;
   end if;
end;

     - Fire in Enter-Query Mode                      Yes
     - Execution Hierarchy                           Override
     * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                    Yes
     - 'Keyboard Help' Text                          
     - Trigger Steps                                 
     ----------
     * Name                                          PRE-INSERT
     - Subclass Information                          
     - Comments                                      
     - Trigger Style                                 PL/SQL
     * Trigger Text

/* Set the date/user created/modified items to the system date/oracle user */
BEGIN
   :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO := sf_get_next_fcl_no(:WB_HAULER_HDR.ORIGIN, :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_DATE);
  --copy(sf_get_waybill_co_no(:WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_DATE,:WB_HAULER_HDR.ORIGIN,:WB_HAULER_HDR.DESTINATION), 'WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO');
  copy(SYSDATE, 'WB_HAULER_HDR.DT_CREATED');
  copy(name_in('PARAMETER.CGU$USER'), 'WB_HAULER_HDR.CREATED_BY');
END;

BEGIN
   if :wb_hauler_hdr.container_company is not null then
      select name
      into   :wb_hauler_hdr.container_company_name 
      from   wb_shipping_companies
      where  code = :wb_hauler_hdr.container_company;
   end if;
EXCEPTION
   when no_data_found then null;   	
END;

BEGIN
   if :wb_hauler_hdr.vessel_company is not null then
      select name
      into   :wb_hauler_hdr.vessel_company_name 
      from   wb_shipping_companies
      where  code = :wb_hauler_hdr.vessel_company;
   end if;
EXCEPTION
   when no_data_found then null;   	
END;

begin
	 select allow_credit
	 into   :wb_hauler_hdr.shipper_allow_credit
	 from   wb_customer
	 where  code = :wb_hauler_hdr.shipper;
exception
   when no_data_found then null;
end;

begin
	 select allow_credit
	 into   :wb_hauler_hdr.consignee_allow_credit
	 from   wb_customer
	 where  code = :wb_hauler_hdr.consignee;
exception
   when no_data_found then null;
end;

begin
   --if :wb_hauler_hdr.voyage_no is not null then
   select voyage_no, vessel_code, s_voyage_no, etd, eta, vessel_name
	 into   :wb_hauler_hdr.voyage_no, :wb_hauler_hdr.s_vessel_code, :wb_hauler_hdr.s_voyage_no, 
	        :wb_hauler_hdr.voya_etd, :wb_hauler_hdr.voya_eta, 
	        :wb_hauler_hdr.voya_vessel
   from (
	 select d.vessel_name, c.voyage_no, nvl(a.dt_mark_as_sailed, a.etd) etd, nvl(a.dt_mark_as_closed, a.eta) eta, c.dt_created, a.shipping_voyage_no s_voyage_no, a.vessel_code
	 from   wb_voyages a, wb_voyage_loading c, wb_vessels d
	 where  a.vessel_code = d.vessel_code 
   and    c.voyage_no  = a.voyage_no
   and    c.fcl_waybill_no = :wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_no
	 order  by c.dt_created ) 
	 where  rownum = 1;
   --end if;
exception
   when no_data_found then null;
end;

declare
   nRowCount Number;
begin
   --msg_alert ('block stat:' || get_block_property('WB_WAYBILL_HDR', STATUS),'I',FALSE);
   if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', STATUS) in ('NEW', 'CHANGED') then
      if :WB_HAULER_HDR.REFERENCE_NO is not null then
         select count(1) 
         into   nRowCount
         from   WB_HAULER_HDR
         where  WAYBILL_NO = :WB_HAULER_HDR.REFERENCE_NO
         and    STATUS <> 'CN';
         if nRowCount > 0 then
            msg_alert ('Pro-Forma No. is already used.', 'E', TRUE);
         end if;
      end if;
   end if;
end;

declare
   nRowCount Number;
begin
   if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', STATUS) in ('NEW', 'CHANGED') then
      if :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO is not null then
         select count(1) 
         into   nRowCount
         from   WB_HAULER_HDR
         where  WAYBILL_NO = :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO;
         if nRowCount > 0 then
            msg_alert ('Waybill No. is already used.', 'E', TRUE);
         end if;
      end if;
   end if;
end;

begin
   select port_code
   into   :wb_hauler_hdr.origin
   from   wb_employees
   where  code = user;
exception
	 when no_data_found then
      msg_alert ('No Port/Location assigned to you. Please contact your supervisor.', 'E', TRUE);
end;

/* CGLY$WHEN_BUTTON_PRESSED */
/* Replicate default menu functionality */
BEGIN
  IF (name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_RECORD') <> name_in('SYSTEM.MOUSE_RECORD'))
  THEN
    go_record(name_in('SYSTEM.MOUSE_RECORD'));
  END IF;
  go_item('WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_DATE');
  do_key('List_values');
END;

       ----------
       * Name                                        WHEN-LIST-CHANGED
       - Subclass Information                        
       - Comments                                    
       - Trigger Style                               PL/SQL
       * Trigger Text                                

begin
   if :wb_hauler_hdr.payment_mode = 'AD' and 
   	  :wb_hauler_hdr.consignee_allow_credit <> 'Y' 
   then
      :wb_hauler_hdr.payment_mode := 'PD';
      msg_alert ('Consignee not allowed for credit transaction.', 'E', TRUE);
   elsif :wb_hauler_hdr.payment_mode = 'AO' and 
   	  :wb_hauler_hdr.shipper_allow_credit <> 'Y' 
   then
      :wb_hauler_hdr.payment_mode := 'PO';
      msg_alert ('Shipper not allowed for credit transaction.', 'E', TRUE);
   end if;    
end;

/* CGUV$CHK_KEYS_ON_VAL_FLD */
/* Check item value against unique or primary key */
BEGIN
  IF :wb_hauler_hdr.payment_mode in ('AO', 'PO') THEN
     sp_get_fcl_rate(:wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_date, :wb_hauler_hdr.container_size, :wb_hauler_hdr.container_type, 
                     :wb_hauler_hdr.origin, :wb_hauler_hdr.destination, :wb_hauler_hdr.service_mode,
                     :wb_hauler_hdr.shipper, :wb_hauler_hdr.rate, :wb_hauler_hdr.rate_eff_date);
  ELSE
     sp_get_fcl_rate(:wb_hauler_hdr.waybill_date, :wb_hauler_hdr.container_size, :wb_hauler_hdr.container_type, 
                     :wb_hauler_hdr.origin, :wb_hauler_hdr.destination, :wb_hauler_hdr.service_mode,
                     :wb_hauler_hdr.consignee, :wb_hauler_hdr.rate, :wb_hauler_hdr.rate_eff_date);
  END IF;

  :wb_hauler_hdr.amt := :wb_hauler_hdr.rate;
  IF :wb_hauler_hdr.amt = -1 THEN
     :wb_hauler_hdr.rate := 0;
     :wb_hauler_hdr.amt := 0;
     msg_alert('WARNING - No rates available for customer ' || :wb_hauler_hdr.shipper || '.', 'W', FALSE);
  END IF;
END;

       * Fire in Enter-Query Mode                    No
       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  Yes
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps

     ----------
     * Name                                          CONTAINER_CODE2
     * Item Type                                     Push Button

     - Help Book Topic

  do_key('List_values');

/* CGFK$VALDIDATE_FK_OVF */
/* Check that foreign key value exists in referenced table */
BEGIN
  IF (
        (name_in('WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE(
        :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE);   /* IN : Value in item :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This Vessel does not exist');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN TOO_MANY_ROWS THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: Value entered does not uniquely define a record');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
  END IF;
END;

/* CGFK$VALDIDATE_FK_OVF */
/* Check that foreign key value exists in referenced table */
BEGIN
  IF (
        (name_in('WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE(
        :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE);   /* IN : Value in item :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This Vessel does not exist');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN TOO_MANY_ROWS THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: Value entered does not uniquely define a record');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
  END IF;
END;

       - Execution Hierarchy                         Override
       * Display in 'Keyboard Help'                  Yes
       - 'Keyboard Help' Text                        
       - Trigger Steps

     * Item Type                                     Display Item

  IF (
        (name_in('WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE') IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    BEGIN
      CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE(
        :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE);   /* IN : Value in item :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE */
    EXCEPTION
      WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: This Vessel does not exist');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN TOO_MANY_ROWS THEN
        MESSAGE('Error: Value entered does not uniquely define a record');
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      WHEN OTHERS THEN
        CGTE$OTHER_EXCEPTIONS;
    END;
  END IF;
END;

/* CGLY$WHEN_BUTTON_PRESSED */
/* Replicate default menu functionality */
declare
   vRepNm    VARCHAR2(60):='WBST0030R.rdf';
   vFileNm   VARCHAR2(64);
   repid      REPORT_OBJECT;  
   v_rep      VARCHAR2(100);  
   rep_status VARCHAR2(32);  
BEGIN  
   if (:WB_HAULER_HDR.CONTAINER_CODE is null) then 
     msg_alert('ERROR - Incomplete details for this waybill.', 'E', TRUE);
   end if;

   BEGIN
      vFilenm := lower('WBST0030R') || '_' || to_char(sysdate,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS')|| '.pdf';
      repid := find_report_object('WBST0030R'); 
      if ID_NULL(repid) then
         msg_alert ('Report not found - please contact ur application developer.', 'E', TRUE);
      end if;
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_FILENAME, sf_get_app_dir || vRepNm ); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_DESNAME, sf_get_scratchpad_dir || vFilenm); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_SERVER, sf_get_report_server); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_OTHER,' paramform=no ' || 
                                                     ' p_waybill_no=' || :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO
                                ); 
      v_rep := RUN_REPORT_OBJECT(repid);  
      rep_status := REPORT_OBJECT_STATUS(v_rep);  
      WHILE rep_status in ('RUNNING','OPENING_REPORT','ENQUEUED') 
      LOOP 
         rep_status := report_object_status(v_rep); 
      END LOOP; 
      IF rep_status = 'FINISHED' THEN 
         web.show_document(sf_get_url || sf_get_scratchpad_url || vFilenm );
      ELSE  
         msg_alert ('Unable to RUN Report - ' || vRepNm || ' - ' || rep_status , 'E', true);
      END IF;  
   END;

END;

declare
   vRepNm    VARCHAR2(60):='WBST0030R.rdf';
   vFileNm   VARCHAR2(64);

   repid      REPORT_OBJECT;  
   v_rep      VARCHAR2(100);  
   rep_status VARCHAR2(32);  

BEGIN  
   if (:WB_HAULER_HDR.CONTAINER_CODE is null) then 
     msg_alert('ERROR - Incomplete details for this waybill.', 'E', TRUE);
   end if;
   if :WB_HAULER_HDR.PRINTED_DT is null then
      :WB_HAULER_HDR.PRINTED_DT := sysdate;
      if :System.Form_Status = 'CHANGED' then Commit_Form; end if;
   end if;
   if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED )='TRUE' then
      set_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED, PROPERTY_FALSE);
   end if;
    
   BEGIN
      vFilenm := lower('WBST0030R') || '_' || to_char(sysdate,'YYYYMMDDHH24MISS')|| '.rrpa';
      repid := find_report_object('WBST0030R'); 
      if ID_NULL(repid) then
         msg_alert ('Report not found - please contact ur application developer.', 'E', TRUE);
      end if;
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_FILENAME, sf_get_app_dir || vRepNm ); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_DESNAME, sf_get_scratchpad_dir || vFilenm); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_SERVER, sf_get_report_server); 
      SET_REPORT_OBJECT_PROPERTY(repid, REPORT_OTHER,' paramform=no ' || 
                                                     ' p_waybill_no=' || :WB_HAULER_HDR.WAYBILL_NO
                                ); 
      v_rep := RUN_REPORT_OBJECT(repid);  
      rep_status := REPORT_OBJECT_STATUS(v_rep);  
      WHILE rep_status in ('RUNNING','OPENING_REPORT','ENQUEUED') 
      LOOP 
         rep_status := report_object_status(v_rep); 
      END LOOP; 
      IF rep_status = 'FINISHED' THEN 
         web.show_document(sf_get_url || sf_get_scratchpad_url || vFilenm );
      ELSE  
         msg_alert ('Unable to RUN Report - ' || vRepNm || ' - ' || rep_status , 'E', true);
      END IF;  
   END;

END;

/* CGLY$WHEN_BUTTON_PRESSED */
/* Replicate default menu functionality */
/* CGLY$WHEN_BUTTON_PRESSED */
/* Replicate default menu functionality */
DECLARE
   err_txt VARCHAR2(80) := 'Are you sure you want to tag this FCL as delivered?'; 
   al_id ALERT; 
   al_button Number; 
BEGIN
   IF :WB_HAULER_HDR.STATUS = 'AR' then

      al_id := FIND_ALERT('CFG_2BUTTON'); 
      SET_ALERT_PROPERTY(al_id, alert_message_text, err_txt ); 
      al_button := SHOW_ALERT( al_id ); 
   
      if al_button = 88 then
         if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED )='FALSE' then
            set_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED, PROPERTY_TRUE);
         end if;
         :WB_HAULER_HDR.STATUS := 'DR';
         :WB_HAULER_HDR.DELIVERED_BY := user;
         :WB_HAULER_HDR.DT_DELIVERED := sysdate;
      end if;

   ELSE

      msg_alert('Only FCL with status ''Arrived'' can be tag as ''Delivered''!', 'E', TRUE);

   END IF;
   commit;
   if get_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED )='TRUE' then
      set_block_property('WB_HAULER_HDR', UPDATE_ALLOWED, PROPERTY_FALSE);
   end if;

END;

/*CGAP$TEMPLATE_NAMED_ROUTINE*/
PROCEDURE displayCalendar IS
BEGIN
   if Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ) is null then
      date_lov.get_date (sysdate, :system.cursor_item );
   else
      date_lov.get_date (Name_In ( :system.cursor_item ), :system.cursor_item );
   end if;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CLOSE_CURSOR_ITEM_WINDOW
   - Subclass Information                            
   * Comments                                        CG$IGNORE_ON_DESIGN_CAPTURE
   * Program Unit Text                               

PROCEDURE Close_Cursor_Item_Window
IS
BEGIN
   CGNV$. TERMINATE_WINDOW
      ( Get_View_Property
           ( Get_Item_Property
                ( :system.cursor_item, item_canvas ),
             window_name ),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.TRIGGER_ITEM'),
        Name_In('SYSTEM.FORM_STATUS'),
        FALSE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            MSG_ALERT
   - Subclass Information                            
   * Comments                                        CG$IGNORE_ON_DESIGN_CAPTURE
   * Program Unit Text                               

procedure msg_alert(
errm in VARCHAR2,           /* message */
errt in VARCHAR2,           /* message type */
rftf in boolean         /* raise form_trigger_failure ? */
) is      /* message parameters */
/*
* ----------------------------------------------------------------
* CHANGE HISTORY:
* DATE   PERSON      CHANGE
* ------ ----------- ---------------------------------------------
*
*/

alert_is alert;
alert_button number;

BEGIN

     IF (errt = 'F')
     THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_SYSTEM_ERROR');
     ELSIF (errt = 'E')
        THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_ERROR');
        ELSIF (errt = 'W')
           THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_WARNING_A');
              ELSIF (errt = 'I')
                 THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_INFORMATION');
                    ELSIF (errt = '2')
	                	THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_2BUTTON');
				               ELSIF (errt = '3')
        			         THEN alert_is := FIND_ALERT('CFG_3BUTTON');
					                 ELSE MESSAGE(errm);
     end if;

     IF (errt IN ('F','E','W','I'))
     THEN SET_ALERT_PROPERTY(alert_is,ALERT_MESSAGE_TEXT,errm);
          alert_button := SHOW_ALERT(alert_is);
     END IF;

     IF (rftf)
     THEN
       RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
     END IF;


END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE */
/* Validate foreign key value/query lookup data. */
PROCEDURE CGFK$CHK_WB_HAULER_HDR_HAHD_VE(
   P_VESSEL_CODE   IN VARCHAR2   /* Value in item :WB_HAULER_HDR.VESSEL_CODE */
)
IS
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);

  CURSOR C1 IS
    SELECT 'x'
    FROM   WB_VESSELS WB_VESSELS
    WHERE  P_VESSEL_CODE = WB_VESSELS.VESSEL_CODE
    ;
  CURSOR C2 IS
    SELECT 'x'
    FROM   WB_VESSELS WB_VESSELS
    WHERE  (P_VESSEL_CODE = WB_VESSELS.VESSEL_CODE
          OR ( WB_VESSELS.VESSEL_CODE is null
          AND  P_VESSEL_CODE is null))
    ;
BEGIN
  IF (
        (P_VESSEL_CODE IS NOT NULL)
     )
  THEN
    OPEN C1;
    FETCH C1
    INTO  CG$DUMMY;
    IF C1%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C1;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C1;
  ELSE
    OPEN C2;
    FETCH C2
    INTO  CG$DUMMY;
    IF C2%NOTFOUND THEN
      CLOSE C2;
      RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
    END IF;
    CLOSE C2;
  END IF;

END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGUV$CHK_HAHD_PK
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGUV$CHK_HAHD_PK */
PROCEDURE CGUV$CHK_HAHD_PK(
   P_WAYBILL_NO IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Item value */
/* Check uniqueness against primary/unique constraint        */
/* Note : NO_DATA_FOUND exception handled by calling trigger */
  CG$DUMMY VARCHAR2(1);
BEGIN
    DECLARE
      CURSOR C IS
        SELECT  '1'
        FROM    WB_HAULER_HDR
        WHERE   WAYBILL_NO = P_WAYBILL_NO;
    BEGIN
      OPEN C;
      FETCH C
      INTO    CG$DUMMY;
      IF C%NOTFOUND THEN
        CLOSE C;
        RAISE NO_DATA_FOUND;
      END IF;
      CLOSE C;
    END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO */
FUNCTION CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(
   P_SERVER_ERR IN NUMBER        /* Server error message */
  ,P_SERVER_MSG IN VARCHAR2)     /* Server error number  */
RETURN BOOLEAN IS
/* Check and report Primary/Unique Key, Check Constraint and User */
/* Defined Constraint violations                                  */
  constraint_name VARCHAR2(61);  /* Violated constraint */
BEGIN
  /* Check if the error code is one we are interested in */
  IF ( NOT (P_SERVER_ERR IN  (1, 2290) OR
           (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) ) )
  THEN
    RETURN( FALSE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with user defined errors */
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR >= 20000 AND P_SERVER_ERR <= 20999) THEN
    MESSAGE('Error: '||CGTE$STRIP_FIRST_ERROR(P_SERVER_MSG));
    RETURN( TRUE );
  END IF;

  /* Deal with Primary/Unique Key and Check Constraint violations */
  constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(P_SERVER_MSG);
  IF (P_SERVER_ERR = 1) THEN
    IF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same Waybill No.');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'EMPL_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same ');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'CUST_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same ');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'CUST_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same ');
    ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HADT_PK') THEN
      MESSAGE('Error: Row exists already with same Container,Waybill No');
    ELSE
      MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
    END IF;
  ELSIF (P_SERVER_ERR = 2290) THEN
    MESSAGE(P_SERVER_MSG);
  END IF;
  RETURN( TRUE );
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Function
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGTE$WB_HAULER_HDR_ERRORS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGTE$WB_HAULER_HDR_ERRORS */
PROCEDURE CGTE$WB_HAULER_HDR_ERRORS IS
/* Trap errors returning from the server and report in a user friendly manner */
BEGIN
  DECLARE
    err_code        CONSTANT NUMBER         := ERROR_CODE;
    err_type        CONSTANT VARCHAR2(3)    := ERROR_TYPE;
    server_err               NUMBER         := abs(DBMS_ERROR_CODE);
    server_msg               VARCHAR2(2000) := DBMS_ERROR_TEXT;
    constraint_name          VARCHAR2(61);
  BEGIN
    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code IN (40506, 40508, 40509, 40510) ) THEN

      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* Check and report the generic constraint violations */
      IF ( CGTE$CHECK_CONSTRAINT_VIO(server_err, server_msg) ) THEN
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* Check and report the constraint violations specific to this block */
      constraint_name := CGTE$STRIP_CONSTRAINT(server_msg);

      /* FK - Parent key not found */
      IF (server_err = 2291) THEN
        IF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_VOYA_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Voyage No. does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_VESS_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Vessel does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_TRUC_PLATE_NO_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Truck Plate No. does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_TRAI_PLATE_NO_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Trailer Plate No. does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_PORT_ORIGIN_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Origin does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_PORT_DESTINATION_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Destination does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_EMPL_DRIVER_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Driver does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_CUST_SHIPPER_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Shipper does not exist');
        ELSIF (constraint_name = 'HAHD_CUST_CONSIGNEE_FK') THEN
          MESSAGE('Error: This Consignee does not exist');
        ELSE
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;

      /* FK - Child record found */
      IF (server_err = 2292) THEN
        IF (err_code = 40510) THEN
          IF (constraint_name = 'HADT_HAHD_FK') THEN
            MESSAGE('Error: Cannot delete Haulers while dependent Hauler Detail exists');
          ELSE
            MESSAGE(server_msg);
          END IF;
        ELSIF (err_code = 40509) THEN
          MESSAGE(server_msg);
        END IF;
        RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
      END IF;
    END IF;

    IF (err_type = 'FRM' AND
        err_code = 40735  AND
        server_err != 0 ) THEN


      /* Remove recursive errors from the top of the stack */
      WHILE (server_err = 604) LOOP
        CGTE$POP_ERROR_STACK(server_err, server_msg);
      END LOOP;

      /* If error not found, issue default message */
      MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(server_err)||': '||server_msg);
      RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;
    END IF;

    /* If error not found, issue default message */
    MESSAGE(err_type||'-'||to_char(err_code)||': '||ERROR_TEXT);
    RAISE FORM_TRIGGER_FAILURE;

  END;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(
   P_CANVAS_LIST    IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* List of displayed canvases */
  ,P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN     VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas             */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN     VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas                */
/* Display the current canvas plus any others in the canvas list */
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);  /* List of displayed canvases */
  canvas_to_raise VARCHAR2(255);  /* Canvas to raise to the top */
BEGIN
  IF ( P_CURRENT_CANVAS = P_BASE_CANVAS) THEN
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  ELSE
    P_CANVAS_LIST := replace(P_CANVAS_LIST, P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',');
    IF ( get_view_property(P_BASE_CANVAS, VISIBLE) = 'FALSE') THEN
      canvas_list := P_CANVAS_LIST;
      WHILE (canvas_list IS NOT NULL) LOOP
        canvas_to_raise := substr(canvas_list, 1, instr(canvas_list, ','));
        canvas_list := replace(canvas_list, canvas_to_raise);
        CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(rtrim(canvas_to_raise, ','), P_BASE_CANVAS);
      END LOOP;
    END IF;
    P_CANVAS_LIST := P_CANVAS_LIST || P_CURRENT_CANVAS || ',';
  END IF;
  CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, P_BASE_CANVAS);
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES */
PROCEDURE CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(
   P_CURRENT_CANVAS IN OUT VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS    IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Find the canvases associated with the current canvas and record which */
/* base canvas is displayed in each window                               */
BEGIN
  /* CFLT */
  P_BASE_CANVAS := P_CURRENT_CANVAS;
  IF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'DATE_LOV_WINDOW') THEN
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWDATE_LOV_WINDOW_PAGE');
  ELSIF (get_view_property(P_CURRENT_CANVAS, WINDOW_NAME) = 'WINDOW') THEN
    copy(P_BASE_CANVAS, 'CG$CTRL.CG$WINDOWWINDOW_PAGE');
  END IF;
END;

   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS */
PROCEDURE CGLY$RAISE_CANVAS(
   P_CANVAS      IN VARCHAR2      /* Current canvas */
  ,P_BASE_CANVAS IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Base canvas    */
/* Raise the current canvas, plus any dependant canvases to the top */
BEGIN
  set_view_property(P_CANVAS, VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  IF ( P_BASE_CANVAS = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
    set_view_property('CG$STACKED_HEADER_1', VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT */
PROCEDURE CGLY$CANVAS_MANAGEMENT IS
/* Top level canvas management procedure */
  current_canvas VARCHAR2(61) := get_item_property(name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_ITEM'), ITEM_CANVAS);
  base_canvas VARCHAR2(61);
  canvas_list VARCHAR2(255);
BEGIN
  IF ( (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') IS NULL) OR (name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS') != current_canvas) ) THEN
    copy(current_canvas, 'CG$CTRL.CG$LAST_CANVAS');
    set_window_property( get_view_property( current_canvas, WINDOW_NAME ), VISIBLE, PROPERTY_ON);
    CGLY$GET_RELATED_CANVASES(current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      canvas_list := name_in('CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
    CGLY$DISPLAY_CANVASES(canvas_list, current_canvas, base_canvas);
    IF ( base_canvas = 'CG$PAGE_1') THEN
      copy(canvas_list, 'CG$CTRL.CG$PAGE_1_LIST');
    END IF;
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$TOGGLE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$TOGGLE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$TOGGLE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN OUT VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Toggle query mode between BSMON and BSMOFF, set all query mode items, */
/* display query mode message, set the relations and ensure that the     */
/* canvas is coordinated.                                                */
BEGIN
  /* Toggle the mode */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE != 'A') THEN
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'A';
  ELSE
    P_QUERY_MODE := 'N';
  END IF;
  /* Set all the items */
  CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Display query mode messages */
  CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* Set the relations */
  CGBS$.SET_RELATIONS( P_QUERY_MODE );
  /* If the query mode is AutoQuery, coordinate outstanding blocks */
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    CGBS$.COORD_VISIBLE_BLKS( name_in('SYSTEM.CURSOR_BLOCK') );
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$SET_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Set all query items to the current query mode */
BEGIN
  NULL;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE */
PROCEDURE CGBS$MESSAGE_QUERY_MODE(
   P_QUERY_MODE IN VARCHAR2) IS  /* Query Mode */
/* Send a message to the status line indicating the current query mode */
BEGIN
  IF (P_QUERY_MODE = 'A') THEN
    NULL;
  ELSE
    MESSAGE('Auto-query mode off');
  END IF;
END;
   * Program Unit Type                               Procedure
   ----------
   * Name                                            CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS
   - Subclass Information                            
   - Comments                                        
   * Program Unit Text                               

/* CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS */
PROCEDURE CGDV$POPULATE_DYNAMIC_LISTS IS
/* Read each lists values from its record group and populate the list */
  temp NUMBER;  /* Return value of populate_group call */
  rg_id RECORDGROUP;  /* Return value of populate_group call */
BEGIN
  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''SERVICE_MODE'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_HAULER_HDR.SERVICE_MODE', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''PAYMENT_MODE'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_HAULER_HDR.PAYMENT_MODE', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''CONTAINER_SIZE'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_HAULER_HDR.CONTAINER_SIZE', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);

  rg_id := create_group_from_query('CGDV$DLRG',
    'SELECT RV_MEANING, RV_LOW_VALUE '||
    'FROM   CG_REF_CODES '||
    'WHERE  RV_DOMAIN = ''WB_WAYBILL_HDR.PAYMENT_STATUS'' '||
    'ORDER BY  1');
  temp := populate_group(rg_id);
  populate_list('WB_HAULER_HDR.PAYMENT_STATUS', rg_id);
  delete_group(rg_id);


END;

       CUST.CONTACT_TITLE CONTACT_TITLE,
       CUST.ADDRESS_1 ADDRESS_1,
       CUST.CONTACT_NO_1 CONTACT_NO_1,
       CUST.EMAIL_ADDRESS EMAIL_ADDRESS,
       CUST.ALLOW_CREDIT
FROM   WB_CUSTOMER CUST
WHERE  CUST.CUSTOMER_TYPE <> 'CONSIGNEE'
UNION
SELECT CUST.CODE CODE,
       CUAL.CUST_ALIAS CUST_ALIAS,
       CUST.COMPANY_NAME COMPANY_NAME,
       CUST.CONTACT_PERSON CONTACT_PERSON,
       CUST.CONTACT_TITLE CONTACT_TITLE,
       CUST.ADDRESS_1 ADDRESS_1,
       CUST.CONTACT_NO_1 CONTACT_NO_1,
       CUST.EMAIL_ADDRESS EMAIL_ADDRESS,
       CUST.ALLOW_CREDIT
FROM   WB_CUSTOMER CUST, WB_CUSTOMER_ALIAS CUAL 
WHERE  CUST.CUSTOMER_TYPE <> 'CONSIGNEE'
AND    CUST.CODE = CUAL.CUST_CODE
ORDER  BY 3
